<body lang=PT-BR style='tab-interval:36.0pt'>

<div class=Section1>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><u><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>RESOLUÇÃO Nº<span class=GramE><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><span style='mso-no-proof:yes'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span></span></span><span style='mso-no-proof:yes'>081/85
- CEP<o:p></o:p></span></span></u></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:8.0cm;text-align:justify'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:
yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:8.0cm;text-align:justify'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:
yes'>Aprova Currículo do Curso de Zootecnia.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>Considerando
o contido no Processo nº 1008/77;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:36.0pt'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>O CONSELHO DE ENSINO, PESQUISA E EXTENSÃO ARPOVOU E EU,
REITOR, SANCIONO A SEGUINTE RESOLUÇÃO:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>Artigo 1º -
Fica aprovado o Currículo do Curso de Zootecnia, conforme consta nos anexos I,
II, III, IV, V, VI e VII, que passam a fazer parte integrante desta Resolução.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:36.0pt'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Artigo 2º - Esta Resolução entra em vigor nesta data, revoga
das <span class=GramE>as</span> disposições em contrário.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:36.0pt'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Dê-se ciência.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:36.0pt'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Cumpra-se.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:8.0cm;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Maringá, 03 de junho de 1985.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:8.0cm;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:8.0cm;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Paulo Roberto Pereira de Souza<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:252.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>REITOR</span></b></p>

<span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-fareast-font-family:
"Times New Roman";color:black;mso-ansi-language:PT-BR;mso-fareast-language:
PT-BR;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA;mso-no-proof:yes'><br clear=all style='page-break-before:
always'>
</span>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><u><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>MATÉRIAS OBRIGATÓRIAS DO CURRÍCULO MÍNIMO E
SEUS DESDOBRAMENTOS EM DISCIPLI­NAS NO CURRÍCULO PLENO<o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><u><span

color:black;mso-ansi-language:PT-BR;mso-fareast-language:PT-BR;mso-bidi-language:
AR-SA;mso-no-proof:yes'><br clear=all style='page-break-before:always'>
</span>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>A N E X O<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>    </span>I I <o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><u><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>DICIPLINAS ADICIONAIS OBRIGATÓRIAS DO
CURRÍCULO PLENO DO CURSO DE ZOOTECNIA<o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><u><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p><span style='text-decoration:none'>&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><u><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p><span style='text-decoration:none'>&nbsp;</span></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>- Introdução à
Zootecnia <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>- Endocrinologia dos
Animais Domésticos <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>- Tecnologia dos
Produtos de Origem Animal <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>- Trabalho de
Graduação<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:black;mso-ansi-language:PT-BR;mso-fareast-language:PT-BR;mso-bidi-language:
AR-SA;mso-no-proof:yes'><br clear=all style='page-break-before:always'>
</span>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>A N E X O<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> 
</span>III<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><u><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>DISCIPLINAS ADICIONAIS OPTATIVAS DO
CURRÍCULO PLENO DO CURSO DE ZOOTECNIA<o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>-
Animais de Biotério<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;

Silvestres<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;

Produção de Couro e Pele - Linguagem de Programação<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>-
Contabilidade Agropecuária - Helicicultura<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>-
Criação de Cães e Gatos<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>A N E X O<span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>      </span>V I I<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><u><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>EMENTAS DAS DISCIPLINAS DO CURRÍCULO PLENO
DO CURSO DE ZOOTECNIA<o:p></o:p></span></u></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'>01.<span style='mso-tab-count:1'>       </span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>Matemática CA</b> (21545)<b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>:</b><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>Cálculo Diferencial e Integral. Noções de
álgebra linear e de geometria analítica<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'>02.<span style='mso-tab-count:1'>       </span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>Química Geral e Inorgânica</b>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>Tabela periódica. Ligações químicas.
Funções Inorgânicas. Estequiometria. Soluções. Equilíbrio químico.
Eletroquímica. Termoquimica. Termodinâmica química<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'>03.<span style='mso-tab-count:1'>       </span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>Citologia</b>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>Morfologia e fisiologia celular. Composição
química da célula. Reprodução e diferenciação celular.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'>04.<span style='mso-tab-count:1'>       </span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'> Zoologia Aplicada à Zootecnia:<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>Conceitos
gerais de zoologia. Estudos de grupos animais de interesse <span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>        </span>agropecuário.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'>05.<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>       </span>Física Geral:<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>Introdução à
termodinâmica. Mecânica. Calorimetria. Ótica. Introdução ao <span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>    </span>eletromagnetismo. Eletricidade. Introdução à
física atômica e nuclear.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'>06.<span style='mso-tab-count:1'>       </span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>Introdução à Zootecnia:</b><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>Importância
social da Zootecnia. Estrutura curricular e Universitária. <span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>   </span>Nomenclatura, origem e domesticação das
espécies domésticas.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'>07.<span style='mso-tab-count:1'>       </span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>Estatística Experimental CA:<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>Noções de
probabilidade. Estatística descritiva. Inferência estatística. <span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>           </span>Análise de regressão. Análise de
variância.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'>08.<span style='mso-tab-count:1'>       </span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>Química Orgânica CA<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>Estrutura e
função dos compostos orgânicos e suas propriedades físicas <span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>     </span>e químicas. Isomeria. Mecanismo de reações
envolvendo alcanos, <span style='mso-tab-count:1'>      </span>cicloalcanos,
alcenos, alcinos, alcadienos, benzeno, fenóis, álcoois, <span style='mso-tab-count:
1'>          </span>haletos, aldeídos, cetonas, ácido carboxilicos e derivados.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-no-proof:yes'>09.<span style='mso-tab-count:1'>       </span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>Química Analítica CA:<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-no-proof:yes'>Princípios <span class=GramE>gerais<span
style='mso-no-proof:no'> Química Analítica</span></span></span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Quantitativa: gravimetria e volumetria. Noções gerais de
Espectrofotometria e Potenciometria.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>10.<span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>       </span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>Iniciação
à Computação:<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Formas de reprodução do pensamento lógico, sua programação
em computa­dores e a <span class=GramE>implementação</span> com a utilização de
uma linguagem para microcomputadores.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>11.<span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>       </span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>Meteorologia</b>
(11435)<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>:</b><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Elementos de Meteorologia básica. <span class=GramE>Fundamentos
